This review was written entirely without invitation or incentive from G2, a seller, or an affiliate." aria-describedby="q7p9hh-tooltip" data-yeti-box="q7p9hh-tooltip" data-toggle="q7p9hh-tooltip" data-resize="q7p9hh-tooltip" data-tooltip="iafvdy-tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-1"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2023-03-23" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2023-03-23">Mar 23, 2023</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-7860499"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Commission Junction stole our deposit and never give it back (6500$)"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">If you want to develop your business via affiliation, make your own affiliation program and develop it yourself by contacting directly the sites that are in your niche. Entrusting this task to Commission Junction and Advertising Purple is simply a huge waste of time and money. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">This whole sad story started with Advertising Purple contacting us with the promise of growing our online business through affiliate marketing with Commission Junction.  Advertising Purple claims to be the company with the largest number of affiliates in the U.S... something no one can verify and after this unfortunate experience is most likely false.  The cost of working with Advertising Purple + Commission Junction is very high between fixed and recurring fees. You have to pay between $5000 and $10,000 just to cover the future commissions of your future affiliates.  Here's how it really works:  Advertising Purple assigns you an account manager who only publishes your site on bogus coupon code and discount sites. The result is that even your customers who don't normally use coupon codes end up on these sites and ultimately make you lose money because without these sites, they would have bought at the price without a discount. In addition to not making you any money, you have to pay them a commission of course. All they do is bid on your brand name!  These coupon sites do not acquire new customers for you (or very few) but allow people who already know your brand to get discounts...so really NO interests at all.  Advertising Purple and Commission Junction promise you to be affiliated with quality sites (audience, traffic etc.) but in reality they are not. Their network literally stops at very poor quality sites with no interests. As for the account manager, let's call it "trainee" with 6 months experience, the word is more appropriate.  We have decided to close our account with both Advertising Purple and Commission Junction. We have been waiting for the return of our deposit at Commission Junction for almost a year now, which is about $6500! Commission Junction is literally stealing from its clients by confiscating the deposit that was given to them at the beginning of the contract. What a shame!  We have contacted our law firm to try to get this money back and our case is ongoing...  If you want to develop your business via affiliation, make your own affiliation program and develop it yourself by contacting directly the sites that are in your niche. Entrusting this task to Commission Junction and Advertising Purple is simply a huge waste of time and money. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7860499 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">They solved nothing href="https://www.g2.com/products/cj-affiliate/reviews/cj-affiliate-review-5039520"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Intuitive Affiliate Platform"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">CJ offers an intuitive website that allows affiliate publishers to locate new and existing merchant partners quickly and identify essential details like commissions and contracts within a few taps. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about CJ Affiliate?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The CJ website offers so many features that, at times, loading speeds are slow. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5039520 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering CJ Affiliate:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">As a platform, CJ ticks all of the boxes for publishers and content creators looking for monetization solutions. The site itself is pretty intuitive — not as functional as Rakuten, but far and above a better UX than Impact. The team at CJ can be surly and brusque and often prioritize the needs of its merchants over interactions with its affiliates. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5039520 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is CJ Affiliate solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">CJ solves the problem of identifying high-quality merchants relevant to our publishing space without the hassle of sifting through irrelevant products and services. Some affiliate platforms focus on quantity; however, CJ focuses on quality. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex
